9-32 DECKLISTS
==============



 Posted in **Event Coverage**
 on May 22, 2016 






![](https://media.magic.wizards.com/styles/auth_small/public/images/hero/wizardslogo_thumb.jpg)
By Meghan Wolff and Jacob Van Lunen











After fifteen rounds of swiss, these are the top 32 decks of Grand Prix Charlotte!
